[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/[0m[95mtmpietmax_e[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m -t ghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m reproduce [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing run against the Wireshark BER dissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`handler_ber`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggered an [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer crash indicating a stack-buffer-overflow. The overflow occurs [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring the handling of a “GeneralString” BER element in `packet-ber.c`. [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSpecifically, `dissect_ber_GeneralString` writes one byte outside the bounds of a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocal buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`name_string`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allocated in the stack frame of [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`try_dissect_unknown_ber`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz-testing of the BER dissector entry point, AddressSanitizer reports a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone-byte write past the end of a stack-allocated buffer. The faulty write [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginates in `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and propagates up [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough `try_dissect_unknown_ber` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.[0m[1;92mc:814[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m825[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The crash is classified [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas a stack-buffer-overflow.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Stack-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, detected by AddressSanitizer, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating out-of-bounds access on a stack buffer.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer ran the `handler_ber` harness with a single seed input, iterating [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m times, and immediately reproduced the overflow.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack frame for `try_dissect_unknown_ber` contains a local array [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string` spanning bytes [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m240[0m[39m. The overflow write lands at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderflowing that array.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash stack trace:  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `dissect_ber_GeneralString` calls code that writes into `name_string` without[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madequate bounds checking.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Fallback logic in `try_dissect_unknown_ber` invokes [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_GeneralString` when an unknown BER tag is encountered.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • AddressSanitizer’s shadow-byte output confirms a “partially addressable” write [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjust outside the buffer’s redzone.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The function `dissect_ber_GeneralString` in `epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mespecially the buffer write logic at line ~[0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The calling context in `try_dissect_unknown_ber` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m814[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m825[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string` is declared and passed to the string-dissection routines.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Any length calculation or boundary checks applied to BER string types, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparticularly GeneralString.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Related ASN.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m context initialization and tag-dispatch code paths in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-ber.c` that may bypass safety checks for unknown or variable-length [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3187[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3194[0m                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3187[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3188[0m[39m:            tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3191[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3192[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root cause analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In dissect_ber_GeneralString [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3179[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code uses a signed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m-bit variable [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`int8_t tvb_len`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to read a length byte from the TVB via [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_get_uint8`. If this byte is ≥ [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m, `tvb_len` becomes negative. The subsequent [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcast to `unsigned` in the bounds check and the index `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderflows, writing before the start of the `name_string` stack buffer.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The intended goal is to copy at most `name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes from the TVB subset [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`out_tvb`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into `name_string`, then NUL-terminate.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve existing logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still want to dissect the GeneralString payload into a temporary buffer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string` provided on the stack, copy up to its capacity minus one, then append[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma terminating NUL.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not change any of the BER parsing, tag dispatch, or the fuzzer harness. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWe only harden the length handling in this one path.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed patch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconceptual steps[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Change the storage type for the TVB-derived length from `int8_t` to an [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned, wide enough type [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `guint32` or `gsize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Instead of reading a single byte from the parent TVB at the post-dissection [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset, query the actual remaining length in the subset TVB [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`out_tvb`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m via [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor `[0m[1;35mtvb_captured_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mget a correct, non-negative byte count.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Compute `copy_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mremaining_len, name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, ensuring we never [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceed the buffer or underflow.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Call `[0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to copy [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly `copy_len` bytes.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Null-terminate with `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m`.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. Remove the old pattern that used the signed `tvb_len`, the misleading cast, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the faulty index.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Step-by-step implementation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Locate packet-ber.c around lines [0m[1;36m3176[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     with:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Robust length clamping: never signed, never overflow/underflow *[0m[35m/[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         guint32 remaining = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint32[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         guint32 copy_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mremaining, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint32[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Copy exactly copy_len bytes and terminate *[0m[35m/[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure `#include [0m[32m"tvbuff.h"[0m[39m` or the appropriate header is present to use [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_reported_length_remaining`.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Rationale and validation  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By switching to an unsigned type and querying the TVB subset’s actual [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremaining length, we eliminate any possibility of a negative or out-of-range copy [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `MIN` clamp guarantees we never write more than `name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving the NUL terminator slot.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change is localized; it does not affect other BER dissectors or the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness code. Existing tests and fuzz harnesses will continue to exercise exactly [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same code paths, but without triggering stack underflows.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar clamp patterns already exist in other restricted string dissectors [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., PrintableString, IA5String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in packet-ber.c, so this brings GeneralString in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline with proven safe implementations.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side effects and mitigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no functional change beyond hardening against invalid lengths.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the original code intended to use the single-byte length field rather than [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe subset length, this patch instead uses the actual subset size. This is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantically correct because `dissect_ber_restricted_string` already parsed the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength field and created `out_tvb` of that exact length.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Running the full Wireshark test suite and the existing fuzz harness will [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm both correctness and absence of new crashes.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer run uncovered a stack-buffer-overflow in Wireshark’s BER [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector, specifically in the function `dissect_ber_GeneralString` when it writes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpast the bounds of the local buffer `name_string`. A patch was proposed that [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplaces the original length computation [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing a signed `tvb_len`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a clamped [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned copy length derived from `tvb_reported_length_remaining` and `name_len`. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch, the build fails with an unused-variable error for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_len`.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During fuzzing of the `handler_ber` dissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`packet-ber.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reported a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte stack-buffer-overflow:  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     WRITE of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at [0m[1;36m0x7fff[0m[39m…2bdf[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     #[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m dissect_ber_GeneralString [0m[35m/src/[0m[95mpacket-ber.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m3194:34[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow occurs when writing the NUL terminator into [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, where `tvb_len` is read from the input and may exceed [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash stack shows the flow: `dissect_ber_GeneralString` → [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`try_dissect_unknown_ber` → core dissector machinery → fuzzer entry point.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations from the Crash Log  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `name_string` is a local array in `try_dissect_unknown_ber`, spanning bytes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m underflows this buffer, indicating improper [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds checking.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code uses `tvb_get_uint8` to read a length, then branches on [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len` to clamp the copy size, but still writes [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m` without further checks.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The attempted diff [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m3185[0m[39m of `packet-ber.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m replaces the signed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_len` logic with:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Robust length clamping: never negative or overflow *[0m[35m/[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     guint32 remaining = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint32[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     guint32 copy_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mremaining, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint32[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch removes the previous branches and always clamps to `name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting a single NUL at the end of the copied region.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Post-Patch Build Log  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The compiler emits a fatal error:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/src/.../[0m[95mpacket-ber.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m3177:13[0m[39m: error: unused variable [0m[32m'tvb_len'[0m[39m [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m[[0m[39m-Werror,-Wunused-variable[0m[1;39m][0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       int8_t tvb_len;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               ^~~~~~~[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This indicates that while the patch replaced usage of `tvb_len`, its [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclaration was not removed, causing the build to fail under `-Werror`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The local declaration and size of `name_string` in `try_dissect_unknown_ber` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand its relation to `name_len`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensuring that all uses of `tvb_len` are either removed or refactored [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistently.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verifying that `tvb_reported_length_remaining` is the correct measure for the [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m937[0m[39m:            case BER_UNI_TAG_BMPString:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m938[0m[39m:                offset = [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_octet_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse, &asn1_ctx, tree, tvb, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart_offset, hf_ber_unknown_BMPString, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m939[0m[39m:                break;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m940[0m[39m:            case BER_UNI_TAG_UniversalString:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m941[0m[39m:                offset = [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_octet_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse, &asn1_ctx, tree, tvb, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart_offset, hf_ber_unknown_UniversalString, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m942[0m[39m:                break;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Remove the unused `tvb_len` variable declaration and all references to [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_get_uint8` in the wrapper `dissect_ber_GeneralString`. This eliminates the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munused-variable build error and the original unsafe logic that could overflow the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer or write out‐of‐bounds.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the entire conditional-copy block:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m* old code using tvb_len *[0m[35m/[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         …[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   with a bounds‐checked sequence that:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Queries the actual length of the TVB subset via[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         guint32 remaining = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Clamps it to `name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` using the existing `MIN` macro:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         guint32 copy_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mremaining, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint32[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Copies exactly `copy_len` bytes:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Writes the NUL terminator at `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Verify that the `MIN` macro, `tvb_memcpy`, and `tvb_reported_length_remaining` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare already in scope; no new includes or utility changes are needed.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rebuild under `-Werror` to confirm there are no unused-variable warnings or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother compiler errors.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Run the same AddressSanitizer-enabled fuzz harness to confirm the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-buffer-overflow is resolved.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removing `tvb_len` directly fixes the unused-variable error introduced by the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevious patch.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The new logic follows the pattern used in the core `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mclamping `len` vs. `max_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but adapts it to the wrapper, using the precise [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpayload length [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`remaining`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than an untrusted byte; this prevents both [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflows and underflows.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- We preserve existing functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcopy up to the available content, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNUL‐terminate for display[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without altering the fuzzer harness or utility [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No other parts of the code are modified, so existing callbacks, memory [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement, and error‐handling remain unchanged.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Since this is a minimal, self-contained change in the wrapper, side effects are [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible; fuzz testing will ensure correctness.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRelevant code context [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3176[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* tvb_len is removed *[0m[35m/[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3177[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3178[0m[39m:    offset = [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_restricted_string[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? &out_tvb : [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3179[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3180[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string && out_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3181[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Robust length clamping: never read past the TVB or buffer *[0m[35m/[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3182[0m[39m:        guint32 remaining = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3183[0m[39m:        guint32 copy_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mremaining, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint32[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3184[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3185[0m[39m:        name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3186[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
